<script type="text/javascript">
function hideErrorPopup()
{
	document.getElementById("fp_popupError").style.display = "none";
}
    (function () {

        // NOTE: overriding core method YUI AutoComplete method due to bug in their widget - click events are not
        // handled properly if the geo-suggest is contained within an LI. This updated method ensures the clicked LI
        // is actually and LI in the list of results.
        YAHOO.widget.AutoComplete.prototype._onContainerClick = function(v,oSelf) {
            var elTarget = YAHOO.util.Event.getTarget(v);
            var elTag = elTarget.nodeName.toLowerCase();
            var elIsItem = elTarget.getAttribute("data-item") == "true";
            while(elTarget && (elTag != "table")) {
                switch(elTag) {
                    case "body":
                        return;
                    case "li":
                        if (elIsItem) {
                            // In case item has not been moused over
                            oSelf._toggleHighlight(elTarget,"to");
                            oSelf._selectItem(elTarget);
                            return;
                        }
                    default:
                        break;
                }

                elTarget = elTarget.parentNode;
                if(elTarget) {
                    elTag = elTarget.nodeName.toLowerCase();
                    elIsItem = elTarget.getAttribute("data-item") == "true";
                }
            }
        };

        YAHOO.widget.AutoComplete.prototype._onTextboxBlur = function (v,oSelf) {
            // Don't treat as a blur if it was a selection via mouse click
            if(!oSelf._bOverContainer || (oSelf._nKeyCode == 9)) {
                // Current query needs to be validated as a selection
                if(!oSelf._bItemSelected) {
                    var elMatchListItem = oSelf._textMatchesOption();
                    // Container is closed or current query doesn't match any result
                    if(!oSelf._bContainerOpen || (oSelf._bContainerOpen && (elMatchListItem === null))) {
                        // Force selection is enabled so clear the current query
                        if(oSelf.forceSelection) {
                            oSelf._clearSelection();
                        }
                        // Treat current query as a valid selection
                        else {
                            oSelf.unmatchedItemSelectEvent.fire(oSelf, oSelf._sCurQuery);
                        }
                    }
                    // Container is open and current query matches a result
                    else {
                        // Force a selection when textbox is blurred with a match
                        if(oSelf.forceSelection) {
                            oSelf._selectItem(elMatchListItem);
                        }
                    }
                } 

                 
                oSelf._clearInterval();
                oSelf._bFocused = false;
                if(oSelf._sInitInputValue !== oSelf._elTextbox.value) {
                    oSelf.textboxChangeEvent.fire(oSelf);
                }
                oSelf.textboxBlurEvent.fire(oSelf);
                if(oSelf._bContainerOpen) {
                    oSelf._toggleContainer(false);
                }
            }
           
           
        };
        
        
        // add an attribute to all LI's to make it easier to detect if correct LI was clicked (works in conjunction
        // with above method _onContainerClick)
        function setCustomAttr (results, container) {
            var listItems = $('li', container),
                i,
                len = listItems.length;

            for (i = 0; i < len; i += 1) {
                listItems[i].setAttribute("data-item", true);
            }

        }

        var AutoComplete = YAHOO.widget.AutoComplete,
            $ = YAHOO.util.Selector.query,
            yuiDom = YAHOO.util.Dom,
            yuiEvent = YAHOO.util.Event,
            yuiSelector = YAHOO.util.Selector,
            sURL = "https://api.starwoodhotels.com/geosuggest?apiKey=fnsxlas9310nndgns9smtinftrpqsnm1&v=2",
            dataSource = new YAHOO.util.ScriptNodeDataSource(sURL),
            hasProp = false,
            hasLocation = false,
            container = $('#' + 'ysearchcontainer', null, true),
            typeInput = $('#' + 'ysearchinput_searchType', null, container),
            propIdsInput = $('#' + 'ysearchinput_propertyIds', null, container),
            geoSuggest;

        dataSource.scriptCallbackParam = "callback";
        dataSource.responseType = YAHOO.util.DataSource.TYPE_JSON;
        dataSource.scriptQueryAppend = "reqRecords=20&localeCode=en_US&brandCode=SPG&options=M";
        dataSource.maxCacheEntries = 100;

        dataSource.responseSchema = {
            resultsList: "ResultSet.Result",
            fields: [ "Title", "Type", "ID" ],
            metaFields: {
                totalRecords: "ResultSet.totalResultsReturned"
            }
        };
        geoSuggest = new AutoComplete("ysearchinput", "ysearchcontainer", dataSource);
        geoSuggest.resultTypeList = false;
        geoSuggest.queryMatchContains = true;
        geoSuggest.useShadow = false;
        geoSuggest.minQueryLength = 2;
        geoSuggest.queryDelay = 0.1;
        geoSuggest.maxResultsDisplayed = 20;
        geoSuggest.animSpeed = 0.0;
        geoSuggest.autoSnapContainer = false;

        geoSuggest.textboxKeyEvent.subscribe(function () {
            // on key up, clear out fields. These should only have values when selecting an item from the list``
            typeInput.value = "";
            propIdsInput.value = "";
        });
        geoSuggest.textboxFocusEvent.subscribe(function () {
            var input = $('#' + 'ysearchinput', null, container);
            // "select" needs to run after current event queue is complete, setTimeout gets this done
            setTimeout(function () {
                input.select();
            }, 0);
        });

        geoSuggest.itemSelectEvent.subscribe(function (a, params) {
            var data = params[2],
                type = data.Type,
                id = data.ID;

            typeInput.value = type;
            if (type == "prop") {
                propIdsInput.value = id;
            }
        });

        geoSuggest.containerCollapseEvent.subscribe(function (a, params) {
            var yuiDom = YAHOO.util.Dom;
            var labels = yuiDom.getElementsByClassName("labelFindHotel");
            for(var i=0; i<labels.length; i++){
                labels[i].className = "labelFindHotel";
            }
        });

        // NOTE: formatResult is called in reverse order on the list of results!
        geoSuggest.formatResult = function (oResultItem, sQuery, sResultMatch) {
            var n = sResultMatch.toLowerCase().indexOf(sQuery.toLowerCase()),
                sStart = sResultMatch.substr(0, n),
                sMatch = sResultMatch.substr(n, sQuery.length),
                sRemainder = sResultMatch.substr(n + sQuery.length),
                aMarkup,
                yuiDom = YAHOO.util.Dom;

            var labels = yuiDom.getElementsByClassName("labelFindHotel");
            for(var i=0; i<labels.length; i++){
                if( labels[i].className.indexOf('openResults') === -1 ) {
                    labels[i].className = labels[i].className + " openResults";
                }

            }

            // open a <div> tag if needed
            if (!hasProp && oResultItem.Type == "prop") {
                hasProp = true;
                aMarkup = "<div>";
            } else if (hasProp && !hasLocation && oResultItem.Type == "location") {
                aMarkup = "<div class='lastLocation'>"
            } else {
                aMarkup = "<div>"
            }

            // output title, bolding matched characters
            if (n >= 0) {
                aMarkup += sStart +
                        "<span style='font-weight:bold'>" +
                        sMatch +
                        "</span>" +
                        sRemainder;
            } else {
                aMarkup += sResultMatch;
            }

            // close any </div> tag if needed
            aMarkup += "</div>";
            if (!hasLocation && oResultItem.Type == "location") {
                hasLocation = true;
            }
            return (aMarkup);
        };
        
            
                function positionResults (textbox, container) {
                    var pos = yuiDom.getXY(textbox);
                    pos[0] += -7;
                    pos[1] += 5;
                    yuiDom.setXY(container, pos);
                    hasProp = false;
                    hasLocation = false;
                }
        function setClassNames (results, container) {
                    var listItems = $('li', container),
                        result,
                        icon = "",
                        lastType = null,
                        firstProp = false,
                        firstLoc = false,
                        i,
                        len = results.length;

                    for (i = 0; i < len; i += 1) {
                        result = results[i];
                        icon = "";
                        firstProp = result.Type == "prop" && lastType != "prop";
                        firstLoc = result.Type == "location" && lastType != "location";
                        if (firstLoc) {
                            icon = "\ue00e";

                        } else if (firstProp) {
                            icon = "\ue011";
                        }
                        listItems[i].setAttribute("data-icon", icon);
                        lastType = result.Type;
                    }

                }
                geoSuggest.doBeforeExpandContainer = function (textbox, container, query, results) {
                    // positionResults() places the geoSuggest drop-down slightly above the text input
                    // for brands that require different positioning, set useGeoSuggestJsPositioning=false and use css styling
                    
                        positionResults(textbox, container);
                    
                    setClassNames(results, container);
                    setCustomAttr(results, container);
                    return true;
                };
            
            
        


    	var geoSearchIcon = yuiDom.getElementsByClassName('geoIconSearch');
	    yuiEvent.addListener(geoSearchIcon, 'click', function(){
	       this.nextElementSibling.focus();
	    });
    })();
</script>
                        </div>

<script type="text/javascript">
var langWatcherTop = {};
langWatcherTop.watching = false;

(function($) {
    $('body').on('click', function(e) {
        if (langWatcherTop.watching) { toggleLanguageMenuTop(); }
    }); 

    $('#layoutHeader .dhtmlSelectTriggerTop').on('click', function(e) {
    	e.stopPropagation();
        toggleLanguageMenuTop();
    });
})(jQuery);

function toggleLanguageMenuTop() {
	if (!$('#layoutHeader #languageSelectorTop').hasClass('show')) {
        $('#layoutHeader #languageSelectorTop').addClass('show');
        langWatcherTop.watching = true;
    } else {
        $('#layoutHeader #languageSelectorTop').removeClass('show');
        langWatcherTop.watching = false;
    }
}
</script>
